# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

## #1

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Instant Hack
    - Three times a run you can add 20 to a Hacking check. Each time you finish a Hack successfully gain 1000 Essence and a random piece of gear with +3 Luck.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Pirate)

## #2

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Blue Buff
    - G = The amount of Blue pieces of gear you have equipped.
    - Defense DC: Gx1.25
    - Armor: Gx1.25
    - Inventory Slots: Gx1.5
    - HP: Gx2.5
    - HP Regen: Gx1.25
    - Defense: +1
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Jiyyagan (Survivor/Jungle)

## #3

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Defense Buff
    - At the End Phase of each turn you may take either a +4 Defense DC and +4 Armor against melee attacks or ranged attacks.
    - You may also choose to resist up to 4 stacks of one Status Effect.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

## #4

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Blue Buff
    - G = The amount of Blue pieces of gear you have equipped.

## #5

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Shortcuts
    - Spend:
    - 250 Essence to use all the functions within your Local Node wherever you are (including the Shop; Essence to Credit conversion and vice versa; and Gear Upgrading, Rerolling, and Condensing)
    - 100 Essence to return to your home node even without clearing the node
    - 100 Essence to drop a marker, allowing you to warp back to that node even if it's within a secure sector
    - 50 Essence to get a small preview of what the next node is like
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Rtolkan (Steampunk)

## #6

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Inter-Node Patch-up
    - Heal the party up to 40 HP between each node.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Asticarian (Modern)

## #7

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Passive: Range Buff
    - Your Range stat is x4.
    - Three times per turn you can do a ranged attack aimed at three targets at once.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Asticarian (Modern)

## #8

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Color 2: Red
- Passive: Party Jump
    - Jump ratio is now 1/3. You and anyone in your party can now do a jump attack that does a 2d12 of damage per Energy spent on the attack.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

## #9

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: AOE Buff
    - Your AOE Radius now = Perception x2.5
    - Your AOEs now get a +7 Damage Plus.
    - You can exclude anyone you want from your AOEs.
    - Three times a turn you can either push everyone who got hit by an AOE attack to the tiles right beyond your AOE Radius or pull them as close as they can be to the center of your AOE.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

## #10

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel

- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Jiyyagan (Survivor/Jungle)

- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

## #14

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Resist Effects
    - Whenever you or anyone you choose within 10 tiles of you is pushed or pulled you may reduce it by 10 tiles.
    - Once per turn you may heal up to 8 stacks of any Status Effect (may be split up any way you'd like).
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

## #15

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves your melee or ranged weapon range you may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If you hit you can choose to make them stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or you may choose to move them up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

## #16

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary

- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Shortcuts
    - Spend:
    - 250 Essence to use all the functions within your Local Node wherever you are (including the Shop; Essence to Credit conversion and vice versa; and Gear Upgrading, Rerolling, and Condensing)
    - 100 Essence to return to your home node even without clearing the node
    - 100 Essence to drop a marker, allowing you to warp back to that node even if it's within a secure sector
    - 50 Essence to get a small preview of what the next node is like
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)
